Structure desc      : top-level additive combination, contains transcendental functions cos, 3 additive terms, complex structure (depth 5)
Fitted params       : c0=-1.8126e+00, c1=-5.8366e-01, c2=1.0000e+00, c3=-1.5708e+00, c4=-3.9487e-07, c5=-9.5308e-01
Train NMSE          : 9.12e-16

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO18)
============================================================
GT: -beta*sin(x)*v - omega0**c0*x
Candidate formulas: 61

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(x,v,t)= -0.583656039990477\, v\sin(x)\;-\;1.81264753578235\,x.
\]
So any matching candidate must be exactly “linear in \(x\)” plus “\(v\) times \(\sin(x)\)” (no extra \(t\)-dependence, no extra nonlinear \(x\) or \(v\) dependence, no absolute values, no denominators unless they can be made constant).

Below, for each candidate I check whether all non-GT structures can be eliminated by setting some candidate constants to 0 (or otherwise making them constant), and whether the trig part can be phase-shifted to \(\sin(x)\).

---

### 1. \(c0*x + c1*v*\cos(c2*x+c3) + c4*v*\max(0,c5+\lvert x\rvert)\)
The Max/Abs term cannot be made identically 0 for all real \(x\) unless \(c4=0\). Then we have \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(c2 x+c3)\), which can match the GT by choosing cosine to equal \(-\sin(x)\) (phase shift) and matching coefficients. **Possible.**

### 2. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*x/(c5*v+c6) + c7/(c5*v+c6)\)
To avoid rational dependence on \(v\), must set \(c4=c7=0\). Then reduces to \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 3. \(c0*x + c1*v*x + c2*x^{c3}\lvert v\rvert^{c4} + c5*v\sin(c6*x+c7)\)
Extra terms \(v x\) and \(x^{c3}\lvert v\rvert^{c4}\) must vanish: set \(c1=0, c2=0\). Then \(c0 x + c5 v\sin(c6 x+c7)\). Choose \(c6=1,c7=0\), and match coefficients/sign. **Possible.**

### 4. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v\cos(c5\log(c6\lvert c7 x+c8\rvert+1))\)
The log/abs cosine term cannot become 0 for all \(x\) unless \(c4=0\). Then reduces to \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 5. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v/(c5*x+c6) + c7/(c5*x+c6)\)
To remove \(1/(c5 x+c6)\) dependence, need \(c4=c7=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 6. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4\log(c5*x+1)\)
Log term must vanish: \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 7. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*t + c5\)
GT has no \(t\) or constant offset, so require \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 8. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v*(c5+t)^{c6}\)
Extra \(v\)-term depending on \(t\) must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 9. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*x*\max(0,c5+\lvert x\rvert)\)
Max term must vanish: \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 10. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*x*(c5+v)^{c6}\)
The extra term couples \(x\) and \(v\); GT has no such coupling. Must set \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 11. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*t*(c5+v)^{c6}\)
Extra \(t\)-dependent term must vanish: \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 12. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(c2+x)\)
This is already \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(x+\text{const})\). Since \(\cos(x+\pi/2)=-\sin(x)\), choose \(c2=\pi/2\) and set \(c1=0.583656...\) to get \(-0.583656 v\sin x\). Choose \(c0=-1.812647...\). **Possible.**

### 13. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*x*(c3+v)^{c4} + c5*v\sin(\cdot)\)
Need no constant: \(c1=0\). Need no \(x*(c3+v)^{c4}\) coupling: set \(c2=0\). Then \(c0 x + c5 v\sin(c6 x+c7)\). Choose \(c6=1,c7=0\), match coefficients. **Possible.**

### 14. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v*(c5+x)^{c6}\)
Extra \(v\)-term depends on \(x\) nontrivially; must set \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 15. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v\log(c5\lvert c6 x\rvert+1)\)
Log/abs term must vanish: \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 16. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(\cdot) + c4*v + c5*v\lvert x\rvert^2\)
GT has no plain \(v\) term and no \(v x^2\) term. Set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then \(c0 x + c1 v\cos(\cdot)\). **Possible.**

### 17. \(c0*x + c1*x + c2*v\sin(c3*x+c4)\)
Combine linear \(x\): \((c0+c1)x\). Trig term is already \(v\sin(\cdot)\). Choose \(c3=1,c4=0\), set \(c2=-0.583656...\), and \(c0+c1=-1.812647...\). **Possible.**

### 18. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(c2*x+c3)\)

### 60. Sum of several terms all divided by \((c3 v+c4)\)
GT has no division by an affine function of \(v\). To remove the denominator dependence, you’d need \(c3=0\) so denominator is constant \(c4\neq 0\). But then you still have terms like \(\sin(c1 x+c2)\) and \(v\sin(c1 x+c7)\) and \(v x\) etc; you could zero most coefficients, but you cannot produce simultaneously a linear \(-1.8126 x\) term and a \(-0.583656 v\sin x\) term without leaving everything scaled by \(1/c4\) (which is fine) **and** ensuring the remaining numerator is exactly \(A x + B v\sin x\). This is actually achievable: set \(c0=0\) (remove standalone sin), \(c8=0\) (remove \(v x\)), \(c9\) used? (there is \(c9*x/(c3 v+c4)\) which can provide the linear \(x\) term), and keep \(c6 v\sin(c1 x+c7)\). With \(c3=0\), expression becomes \((c5 x + c6 v\sin(c1 x+c7)+c9 x)/c4\). Choose \(c1=1,c7=0\). Then it is \(((c5+c9)/c4)x + (c6/c4) v\sin x\). Match coefficients by choosing constants. **Possible.**

### 61. Similar structure with denominator \((c3 v+c4)\)
Same reasoning: set \(c3=0\) to make denominator constant; zero unwanted terms; keep \(c5 x\) and \(c6 v\sin(c1 x+c2)\) with \(c1=1,c2=0\). Then match coefficients via scaling by \(1/c4\). **Possible.**

Let me note that `v*cos(x + c)` can become `v*sin(x)` when `c = -π/2` (since `cos(x - π/2) = sin(x)`). So candidates with `c1*v*cos(c2*x + c3)` can match `v*sin(x)` if `c2 = 1` and `c3 = -π/2`.
